  30 | 
  31 | def _concentration_from_column(column_name: str) -> float:
  32 |     """Extract concentration in uM from a response column label."""
  33 |     match = re.search(r":\s*([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)uM\s*$", column_name)
  34 |     if match is None:
  35 |         raise ValueError(f"Could not parse concentration from column: {column_name}")
  36 |     return float(match.group(1))
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def _load_fit_table(data_file: Path = DATA_FILE) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
  40 |     """Load wide fit.tsv and return X=[measurement_x, concentration_uM], y."""
  41 |     features: list[list[float]] = []
  42 |     targets: list[float] = []
  43 | 
  44 |     with data_file.open(newline="") as f:
  45 |         reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter="\t")
  46 |         header = next(reader)
  47 |         concentrations = [_concentration_from_column(name) for name in header[1:]]
  48 | 
  49 |         for row in reader:
  50 |             if not row:
  51 |                 continue
  52 |             measurement_x = float(row[0])
  53 |             for concentration, value in zip(concentrations, row[1:]):
  54 |                 if value == "" or value.strip().lower() == "nan":
  55 |                     continue
  56 |                 features.append([measurement_x, concentration])
  57 |                 targets.append(float(value))
  58 | 
  59 |     if not features:
  60 |         raise ValueError(f"No regression samples loaded from {data_file}")
  61 | 
  62 |     return np.asarray(features, dtype=float), np.asarray(targets, dtype=float)
  63 | 
  64 | 
  65 | def load_alphasyn_data():
  66 |     """Deterministic train/validation split for the copied Alpha-synuclein TSV."""
  67 |     X, y = _load_fit_table()
  68 |     rng = np.random.default_rng(RANDOM_STATE)
  69 |     indices = rng.permutation(len(y))
  70 |     split = int(round(len(y) * (1.0 - TEST_SIZE)))
  71 |     train_idx = indices[:split]
  72 |     val_idx = indices[split:]
  73 |     return X[train_idx], X[val_idx], y[train_idx], y[val_idx]
  74 |

  76 | def evaluate_candidate_with_timeout(program_path: str, timeout_seconds: int = 300) -> dict:
  77 |     """
  78 |     Evaluate a candidate program in a subprocess and return its metrics dict.
  79 | 
  80 |     The candidate's `evaluate_symbolic_candidate()` function is the evolved
  81 |     artifact: it should build an equation template and call the harness evaluator.
  82 |     This function only isolates evaluation behind a timeout; it does not run
  83 |     PySR's search loop.
  84 |     """
  85 |     harness_root = str(BENCHMARK_ROOT)
  86 |     evaluator_path = str(Path(__file__).resolve())
  87 |     with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(suffix=".py", delete=False) as temp_file:

  90 | import pickle

  92 | import traceback

  94 | sys.path.insert(0, {harness_root!r})
  95 |

 112 |         result = program.evaluate_symbolic_candidate(
 113 |             X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val
 114 |         )
 115 |     elif hasattr(program, "run_discovery"):
 116 |         result = program.run_discovery(X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val)
 117 |     else:
 118 |         raise AttributeError("Program must define evaluate_symbolic_candidate() or run_discovery()")
 119 | 
 120 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 121 |         pickle.dump({{"result": result}}, f)
 122 | except Exception as exc:
 123 |     traceback.print_exc()
 124 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 125 |         pickle.dump({{"error": str(exc)}}, f)
 126 | """
 127 |         temp_file.write(script.encode())
 128 |         temp_path = temp_file.name
 129 | 
 130 |     results_path = f"{temp_path}.results"
 131 |     try:
 132 |         process = subprocess.Popen(
 133 |             [sys.executable, temp_path],
 134 |             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
 135 |             stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
 136 |         )
 137 |         stdout, stderr = process.communicate(timeout=timeout_seconds)
 138 |         if stdout:
 139 |             print(stdout.decode())
 140 |         if stderr:
 141 |             print(stderr.decode())
 142 |         if process.returncode != 0:
 143 |             raise RuntimeError(f"Subprocess exited with code {process.returncode}")
 144 |         if not os.path.exists(results_path):
 145 |             raise RuntimeError("Results file not found")
 146 |         with open(results_path, "rb") as f:
 147 |             payload = pickle.load(f)
 148 |         if "error" in payload:
 149 |             raise RuntimeError(payload["error"])
 150 |         return payload["result"]
 151 |     except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
 152 |         process.kill()
 153 |         process.wait()
 154 |         raise TimeoutError(f"Program execution timed out after {timeout_seconds}s")
 155 |     finally:
 156 |         for path in (temp_path, results_path):
 157 |             if os.path.exists(path):
 158 |                 os.unlink(path)

import csv
import numpy as np

with open('alphasyn_gaspar2017_03um_seed_all/fit.tsv') as f:
    reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
    header = next(reader)
    times = []
    rows = []
    for row in reader:
        if row:
            times.append(float(row[0]))
            vals = []
            for v in row[1:]:
                try:
                    vals.append(float(v))
                except:
                    vals.append(np.nan)
            rows.append(vals)

times = np.array(times)
rows = np.array(rows)
print('Time range:', times[0], '-', times[-1])
print('Shape:', rows.shape)
# Find where each concentration crosses 0.5 (half-time)
concs = [1, 2, 3, 5, 10, 20, 30, 50]
for i, c in enumerate(concs):
    col = rows[:, i]
    # Find crossing of 0.5
    idx = np.where(col >= 0.5)[0]
    if len(idx) > 0:
        t_half = times[idx[0]]
        print(f'  C={c}uM: t_half~{t_half:.2f}h, initial={col[0]:.4f}')
    else:
        print(f'  C={c}uM: never reaches 0.5, max={col.max():.4f}')

import csv
import numpy as np

with open('alphasyn_gaspar2017_03um_seed_all/fit.tsv') as f:
    reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
    header = next(reader)
    times = []
    rows = []
    for row in reader:
        if row:
            times.append(float(row[0]))
            vals = []
            for v in row[1:]:
                try:
                    vals.append(float(v))
                except:
                    vals.append(np.nan)
            rows.append(vals)

times = np.array(times)
rows = np.array(rows)

concs = np.array([1, 2, 3, 5, 10, 20, 30, 50])

# The initial value looks like ~ seed_fraction/(seed_fraction + monomer_fraction)
# If seed=0.3uM, monomer=C, then seed/(seed+C) = 0.3/(0.3+C)
print('Predicted y0 = 0.3/(0.3+C):')
for c in concs:
    print(f'  C={c}: {0.3/(0.3+c):.6f}')

print()
print('Actual y0:')
for i, c in enumerate(concs):
    print(f'  C={c}: {rows[0,i]:.6f}')

# Check: seed/(seed+C) where seed=?
# y0 = s/(s+C) => s = y0*C/(1-y0)
s_est = rows[0,:] * concs / (1 - rows[0,:])
print()
print('Estimated seed from y0:', s_est)

  53 | def pysr_operator_namespace() -> dict[str, Any]:
  54 |     """
  55 |     Return PySR-to-SymPy operator callables usable in expression templates.
  56 | 
  57 |     Operators like ``+``, ``-``, ``*``, and ``/`` should be written with normal
  58 |     Python syntax. Named PySR operators such as ``sin``, ``cos``, ``sqrt``,
  59 |     ``log1p``, ``max``, ``min``, ``muladd``, and ``clamp`` are exposed here.
  60 |     """
  61 |     return {
  62 |         **sympy_mappings,
  63 |         "pi": sp.pi,
  64 |         "E": sp.E,
  65 |     }

  68 | def _as_sympy_expr(expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> sp.Expr:
  69 |     if isinstance(expression, sp.Expr):
  70 |         return expression
  71 |     return pysr2sympy(expression, feature_names_in=list(feature_names))
  72 | 
  73 | 
  74 | def _complexity(expression: sp.Expr) -> float:
  75 |     return float(sum(1 for _ in sp.preorder_traversal(expression)))
  76 |

  78 | def _predict(expression: sp.Expr, X: NDArray, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> NDArray:
  79 |     symbols = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
  80 |     fn = sympy2numpy(expression, symbols)
  81 |     with np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
  82 |         if isinstance(fn, CallableEquation):
  83 |             y_pred = fn(np.asarray(X, dtype=float))
  84 |         else:
  85 |             y_pred = fn(*[X[:, i] for i in range(X.shape[1])])
  86 |     return np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).reshape(-1)

  89 | def fit_expression_constants(
  90 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
  91 |     X_train: NDArray,
  92 |     y_train: NDArray,
  93 |     X_val: NDArray,
  94 |     *,
  95 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
  96 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
  97 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
  98 | ) -> FittedExpression:
  99 |     """
 100 |     Fit free constants in a SkyDiscover-proposed expression template.
 101 | 
 102 |     The expression structure is supplied by the evolved program. This helper only
 103 |     performs the continuous inner fit and PySR-style export/evaluation.
 104 |     """
 105 |     X_train = np.asarray(X_train, dtype=float)
 106 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 107 |     X_val = np.asarray(X_val, dtype=float)
 108 |     feature_names = [f"x{i}" for i in range(X_train.shape[1])]
 109 |     template = _as_sympy_expr(expression, feature_names)
 110 | 
 111 |     if constants is None:
 112 |         feature_set = set(feature_symbols(X_train.shape[1]))
 113 |         constants = sorted(template.free_symbols - feature_set, key=lambda s: s.name)
 114 |     constants = list(constants)
 115 | 
 116 |     if not constants:
 117 |         fitted_expr = sp.simplify(template)
 118 |         return FittedExpression(
 119 |             expression_template=template,
 120 |             expression=fitted_expr,
 121 |             constants={},
 122 |             y_pred_train=_predict(fitted_expr, X_train, feature_names),
 123 |             y_pred_val=_predict(fitted_expr, X_val, feature_names),
 124 |         )
 125 | 
 126 |     if initial_values is None:
 127 |         x0 = np.ones(len(constants), dtype=float)
 128 |     else:
 129 |         x0 = np.asarray(initial_values, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 130 |         if x0.size != len(constants):
 131 |             raise ValueError("initial_values must match the number of constants")
 132 | 
 133 |     def residual(theta: NDArray) -> NDArray:
 134 |         substitutions = {symbol: float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, theta)}
 135 |         candidate = template.subs(substitutions)
 136 |         try:
 137 |             prediction = _predict(candidate, X_train, feature_names)
 138 |         except Exception:
 139 |             return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 140 |         if prediction.shape != y_train.shape or not np.all(np.isfinite(prediction)):
 141 |             return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 142 |         return prediction - y_train
 143 | 
 144 |     import warnings
 145 | 
 146 |     with warnings.catch_warnings(), np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
 147 |         warnings.simplefilter("ignore", RuntimeWarning)
 148 |         result = least_squares(
 149 |             residual,
 150 |             x0,
 151 |             loss="soft_l1",
 152 |             max_nfev=max_nfev,
 153 |         )
 154 |     fitted_constants = {
 155 |         str(symbol): float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, result.x)
 156 |     }
 157 |     substitutions = dict(zip(constants, result.x))
 158 |     fitted_expr = sp.simplify(template.subs(substitutions))
 159 | 
 160 |     return FittedExpression(
 161 |         expression_template=template,
 162 |         expression=fitted_expr,
 163 |         constants=fitted_constants,
 164 |         y_pred_train=_predict(fitted_expr, X_train, feature_names),
 165 |         y_pred_val=_predict(fitted_expr, X_val, feature_names),
 166 |     )

 168 | 
 169 | def evaluate_expression(
 170 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
 171 |     X_train: NDArray,
 172 |     y_train: NDArray,
 173 |     X_val: NDArray,
 174 |     y_val: NDArray,
 175 |     *,
 176 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
 177 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
 178 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
 179 | ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 180 |     """Score a proposed equation template after fitting its constants."""
 181 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 182 |     y_val = np.asarray(y_val, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 183 |     fitted = fit_expression_constants(
 184 |         expression,
 185 |         X_train,
 186 |         y_train,
 187 |         X_val,
 188 |         constants=constants,
 189 |         initial_values=initial_values,
 190 |         max_nfev=max_nfev,
 191 |     )
 192 |     nmse_train = nmse(y_train, fitted.y_pred_train)
 193 |     nmse_val = nmse(y_val, fitted.y_pred_val)
 194 |     loss = float(np.mean((fitted.y_pred_train - y_train) ** 2))
 195 | 
 196 |     return {
 197 |         "equation_template": str(fitted.expression_template),
 198 |         "equation": str(fitted.expression),
 199 |         "constants": fitted.constants,
 200 |         "loss": loss,
 201 |         "complexity": _complexity(fitted.expression_template),
 202 |         "nmse_train": nmse_train,
 203 |         "nmse_val": nmse_val,

pysr_harness/metrics.py (lines 1-27 of 27)
   1 | """Shared scoring helpers for symbolic regression benchmarks."""
   2 | 
   3 | from __future__ import annotations
   4 | 
   5 | import numpy as np
   6 | from numpy.typing import NDArray
   7 | 
   8 | 
   9 | def nmse(y_true: NDArray, y_pred: NDArray) -> float:
  10 |     """Normalized mean squared error."""
  11 |     y_true = np.asarray(y_true, dtype=float).ravel()
  12 |     y_pred = np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).ravel()
  13 |     if y_true.shape != y_pred.shape:
  14 |         return float("inf")
  15 |     if not np.all(np.isfinite(y_pred)):
  16 |         return float("inf")
  17 |     var = float(np.var(y_true))
  18 |     if var <= 0.0:
  19 |         return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2))
  20 |     return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2) / var)
  21 | 
  22 | 
  23 | def combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val: float) -> float:
  24 |     """Higher is better; zero for invalid or infinite NMSE."""
  25 |     if not np.isfinite(nmse_val):
  26 |         return 0.0
  27 |     return float(1.0 / (1.0 + max(nmse_val, 0.0)))

  30 | 
  31 | def _concentration_from_column(column_name: str) -> float:
  32 |     """Extract concentration in uM from a response column label."""
  33 |     match = re.search(r":\s*([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)uM\s*$", column_name)
  34 |     if match is None:
  35 |         raise ValueError(f"Could not parse concentration from column: {column_name}")
  36 |     return float(match.group(1))
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def _load_fit_table(data_file: Path = DATA_FILE) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
  40 |     """Load wide fit.tsv and return X=[measurement_x, concentration_uM], y."""
  41 |     features: list[list[float]] = []
  42 |     targets: list[float] = []
  43 | 
  44 |     with data_file.open(newline="") as f:
  45 |         reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter="\t")
  46 |         header = next(reader)
  47 |         concentrations = [_concentration_from_column(name) for name in header[1:]]
  48 | 
  49 |         for row in reader:
  50 |             if not row:
  51 |                 continue
  52 |             measurement_x = float(row[0])
  53 |             for concentration, value in zip(concentrations, row[1:]):
  54 |                 if value == "" or value.strip().lower() == "nan":
  55 |                     continue
  56 |                 features.append([measurement_x, concentration])
  57 |                 targets.append(float(value))
  58 | 
  59 |     if not features:
  60 |         raise ValueError(f"No regression samples loaded from {data_file}")
  61 | 
  62 |     return np.asarray(features, dtype=float), np.asarray(targets, dtype=float)
  63 | 
  64 | 
  65 | def load_alphasyn_data():
  66 |     """Deterministic train/validation split for the copied Alpha-synuclein TSV."""
  67 |     X, y = _load_fit_table()
  68 |     rng = np.random.default_rng(RANDOM_STATE)
  69 |     indices = rng.permutation(len(y))
  70 |     split = int(round(len(y) * (1.0 - TEST_SIZE)))
  71 |     train_idx = indices[:split]
  72 |     val_idx = indices[split:]
  73 |     return X[train_idx], X[val_idx], y[train_idx], y[val_idx]
  74 |

 115 |     elif hasattr(program, "run_discovery"):
 116 |         result = program.run_discovery(X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val)
 117 |     else:
 118 |         raise AttributeError("Program must define evaluate_symbolic_candidate() or run_discovery()")
 119 |

 121 |         pickle.dump({{"result": result}}, f)
 122 | except Exception as exc:
 123 |     traceback.print_exc()
 124 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 125 |         pickle.dump({{"error": str(exc)}}, f)
 126 | """
 127 |         temp_file.write(script.encode())
 128 |         temp_path = temp_file.name
 129 | 
 130 |     results_path = f"{temp_path}.results"
 131 |     try:
 132 |         process = subprocess.Popen(
 133 |             [sys.executable, temp_path],
 134 |             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
 135 |             stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
 136 |         )
 137 |         stdout, stderr = process.communicate(timeout=timeout_seconds)
 138 |         if stdout:
 139 |             print(stdout.decode())
 140 |         if stderr:
 141 |             print(stderr.decode())
 142 |         if process.returncode != 0:
 143 |             raise RuntimeError(f"Subprocess exited with code {process.returncode}")
 144 |         if not os.path.exists(results_path):
 145 |             raise RuntimeError("Results file not found")
 146 |         with open(results_path, "rb") as f:
 147 |             payload = pickle.load(f)
 148 |         if "error" in payload:
 149 |             raise RuntimeError(payload["error"])
 150 |         return payload["result"]
 151 |     except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
 152 |         process.kill()
 153 |         process.wait()
 154 |         raise TimeoutError(f"Program execution timed out after {timeout_seconds}s")
 155 |     finally:
 156 |         for path in (temp_path, results_path):
 157 |             if os.path.exists(path):
 158 |                 os.unlink(path)

 161 | def _metrics_from_result(result: dict, eval_time: float) -> dict:
 162 |     """Normalize harness output into SkyDiscover evaluator metrics."""
 163 |     nmse_val = float(result.get("nmse_val", float("inf")))
 164 |     combined = float(result.get("combined_score", combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val)))
 165 |     if not np.isfinite(combined):
 166 |         combined = 0.0
 167 | 
 168 |     return {
 169 |         "equation": str(result.get("equation", "")),
 170 |         "loss": float(result.get("loss", float("inf"))),
 171 |         "complexity": float(result.get("complexity", 0.0)),
 172 |         "nmse_train": float(result.get("nmse_train", float("inf"))),
 173 |         "nmse_val": nmse_val,
 174 |         "combined_score": combined,
 175 |         "eval_time": float(eval_time),
 176 |     }

 179 | def evaluate(program_path: str) -> dict:
 180 |     """Evaluate one evolved symbolic-equation candidate on the Alpha-synuclein TSV."""
 181 |     try:
 182 |         start = time.time()
 183 |         result = evaluate_candidate_with_timeout(program_path, timeout_seconds=600)

 190 |             f"time={metrics['eval_time']:.2f}s"
 191 |         )
 192 |         print(f"Best equation: {metrics['equation']}")
 193 |         return metrics
 194 |     except Exception as exc:
 195 |         print(f"Evaluation failed: {exc}")
 196 |         traceback.print_exc()

  46 |     kinetic models that fit sigmoidal aggregation curves with concentration dependence.
  47 |

  49 |     Improve the `evaluate_symbolic_candidate()` function in the EVOLVE-BLOCK.
  50 |     Build an explicit symbolic expression template using the `pysr_harness` API.
  51 |

  53 |     - `feature_symbols(n)` → PySR variables `x0`, `x1`, ...

  55 |     - `evaluate_expression(expr, X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val, constants=...)`
  56 |       fits constants via least-squares and returns scored metrics.
  57 | 
  58 |     ## Equation design guidance
  59 |     The sigmoidal curves suggest models like:
  60 |     - Exponential approach: y = 1 - exp(-k*t^n) (Avrami/stretched exponential)
  61 |     - Finke-Watzky: y = (k1/k2)(exp((k1+k2*C)*t)-1) / (1 + (k1/k2)*exp((k1+k2*C)*t))
  62 |     - Logistic/Hill: y = t^n / (t_half^n + t^n) with concentration-dependent t_half
  63 |     - Secondary nucleation: concentration affects both lag time and growth rate
  64 | 
  65 |     The concentration dependence should appear in rate constants, half-times, or
  66 |     exponents — NOT as separate additive terms.

  70 |     - Keep expressions numerically stable and general.
  71 |     - Do not hardcode data values or indices.

  41 |     return [sp.Symbol(f"c{i}", real=True) for i in range(n_constants)]

  46 |     return {
  47 |         "unary": GENERAL_UNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  48 |         "binary": GENERAL_BINARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  49 |         "ternary": GENERAL_TERNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),

  53 | def pysr_operator_namespace() -> dict[str, Any]:
  54 |     """
  55 |     Return PySR-to-SymPy operator callables usable in expression templates.
  56 | 
  57 |     Operators like ``+``, ``-``, ``*``, and ``/`` should be written with normal
  58 |     Python syntax. Named PySR operators such as ``sin``, ``cos``, ``sqrt``,
  59 |     ``log1p``, ``max``, ``min``, ``muladd``, and ``clamp`` are exposed here.
  60 |     """
  61 |     return {
  62 |         **sympy_mappings,
  63 |         "pi": sp.pi,
  64 |         "E": sp.E,
  65 |     }

  68 | def _as_sympy_expr(expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> sp.Expr:
  69 |     if isinstance(expression, sp.Expr):
  70 |         return expression
  71 |     return pysr2sympy(expression, feature_names_in=list(feature_names))
  72 | 
  73 | 
  74 | def _complexity(expression: sp.Expr) -> float:
  75 |     return float(sum(1 for _ in sp.preorder_traversal(expression)))
  76 | 
  77 | 
  78 | def _predict(expression: sp.Expr, X: NDArray, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> NDArray:
  79 |     symbols = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
  80 |     fn = sympy2numpy(expression, symbols)
  81 |     with np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
  82 |         if isinstance(fn, CallableEquation):
  83 |             y_pred = fn(np.asarray(X, dtype=float))
  84 |         else:
  85 |             y_pred = fn(*[X[:, i] for i in range(X.shape[1])])
  86 |     return np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
  87 |

  89 | def fit_expression_constants(
  90 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
  91 |     X_train: NDArray,
  92 |     y_train: NDArray,
  93 |     X_val: NDArray,
  94 |     *,
  95 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
  96 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
  97 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
  98 | ) -> FittedExpression:
  99 |     """
 100 |     Fit free constants in a SkyDiscover-proposed expression template.
 101 | 
 102 |     The expression structure is supplied by the evolved program. This helper only
 103 |     performs the continuous inner fit and PySR-style export/evaluation.
 104 |     """
 105 |     X_train = np.asarray(X_train, dtype=float)
 106 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 107 |     X_val = np.asarray(X_val, dtype=float)
 108 |     feature_names = [f"x{i}" for i in range(X_train.shape[1])]
 109 |     template = _as_sympy_expr(expression, feature_names)
 110 | 
 111 |     if constants is None:
 112 |         feature_set = set(feature_symbols(X_train.shape[1]))
 113 |         constants = sorted(template.free_symbols - feature_set, key=lambda s: s.name)
 114 |     constants = list(constants)
 115 | 
 116 |     if not constants:
 117 |         fitted_expr = sp.simplify(template)
 118 |         return FittedExpression(
 119 |             expression_template=template,
 120 |             expression=fitted_expr,
 121 |             constants={},
 122 |             y_pred_train=_predict(fitted_expr, X_train, feature_names),
 123 |             y_pred_val=_predict(fitted_expr, X_val, feature_names),
 124 |         )
 125 | 
 126 |     if initial_values is None:
 127 |         x0 = np.ones(len(constants), dtype=float)
 128 |     else:
 129 |         x0 = np.asarray(initial_values, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 130 |         if x0.size != len(constants):
 131 |             raise ValueError("initial_values must match the number of constants")
 132 | 
 133 |     def residual(theta: NDArray) -> NDArray:
 134 |         substitutions = {symbol: float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, theta)}
 135 |         candidate = template.subs(substitutions)
 136 |         try:
 137 |             prediction = _predict(candidate, X_train, feature_names)
 138 |         except Exception:
 139 |             return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 140 |         if prediction.shape != y_train.shape or not np.all(np.isfinite(prediction)):
 141 |             return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 142 |         return prediction - y_train
 143 | 
 144 |     import warnings
 145 | 
 146 |     with warnings.catch_warnings(), np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
 147 |         warnings.simplefilter("ignore", RuntimeWarning)
 148 |         result = least_squares(
 149 |             residual,
 150 |             x0,
 151 |             loss="soft_l1",
 152 |             max_nfev=max_nfev,
 153 |         )
 154 |     fitted_constants = {
 155 |         str(symbol): float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, result.x)
 156 |     }
 157 |     substitutions = dict(zip(constants, result.x))
 158 |     fitted_expr = sp.simplify(template.subs(substitutions))
 159 | 
 160 |     return FittedExpression(
 161 |         expression_template=template,
 162 |         expression=fitted_expr,
 163 |         constants=fitted_constants,
 164 |         y_pred_train=_predict(fitted_expr, X_train, feature_names),
 165 |         y_pred_val=_predict(fitted_expr, X_val, feature_names),
 166 |     )
 167 | 
 168 | 
 169 | def evaluate_expression(
 170 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
 171 |     X_train: NDArray,
 172 |     y_train: NDArray,
 173 |     X_val: NDArray,
 174 |     y_val: NDArray,
 175 |     *,
 176 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
 177 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
 178 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
 179 | ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 180 |     """Score a proposed equation template after fitting its constants."""
 181 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 182 |     y_val = np.asarray(y_val, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 183 |     fitted = fit_expression_constants(
 184 |         expression,
 185 |         X_train,
 186 |         y_train,
 187 |         X_val,
 188 |         constants=constants,
 189 |         initial_values=initial_values,
 190 |         max_nfev=max_nfev,
 191 |     )
 192 |     nmse_train = nmse(y_train, fitted.y_pred_train)
 193 |     nmse_val = nmse(y_val, fitted.y_pred_val)
 194 |     loss = float(np.mean((fitted.y_pred_train - y_train) ** 2))
 195 | 
 196 |     return {
 197 |         "equation_template": str(fitted.expression_template),
 198 |         "equation": str(fitted.expression),
 199 |         "constants": fitted.constants,
 200 |         "loss": loss,
 201 |         "complexity": _complexity(fitted.expression_template),
 202 |         "nmse_train": nmse_train,
 203 |         "nmse_val": nmse_val,
 204 |         "combined_score": combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val),
 205 |     }

pysr_harness/metrics.py (lines 1-27 of 27)
   1 | """Shared scoring helpers for symbolic regression benchmarks."""
   2 | 
   3 | from __future__ import annotations
   4 | 
   5 | import numpy as np
   6 | from numpy.typing import NDArray
   7 | 
   8 | 
   9 | def nmse(y_true: NDArray, y_pred: NDArray) -> float:
  10 |     """Normalized mean squared error."""
  11 |     y_true = np.asarray(y_true, dtype=float).ravel()
  12 |     y_pred = np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).ravel()
  13 |     if y_true.shape != y_pred.shape:
  14 |         return float("inf")
  15 |     if not np.all(np.isfinite(y_pred)):
  16 |         return float("inf")
  17 |     var = float(np.var(y_true))
  18 |     if var <= 0.0:
  19 |         return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2))
  20 |     return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2) / var)
  21 | 
  22 | 
  23 | def combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val: float) -> float:
  24 |     """Higher is better; zero for invalid or infinite NMSE."""
  25 |     if not np.isfinite(nmse_val):
  26 |         return 0.0
  27 |     return float(1.0 / (1.0 + max(nmse_val, 0.0)))

alphasyn_gaspar2017_03um_seed_all/evaluator.py (lines 1-247 of 247)
   1 | """Evaluator for Alpha-synuclein Gaspar 2017 0.3uM seed symbolic regression."""
   2 | 
   3 | from __future__ import annotations
   4 | 
   5 | import csv
   6 | import importlib.util
   7 | import os
   8 | import pickle
   9 | import re
  10 | import subprocess
  11 | import sys
  12 | import tempfile
  13 | import time
  14 | import traceback
  15 | from pathlib import Path
  16 | 
  17 | BENCHMARK_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
  18 | BENCHMARK_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]
  19 | if str(BENCHMARK_ROOT) not in sys.path:
  20 |     sys.path.insert(0, str(BENCHMARK_ROOT))
  21 | 
  22 | import numpy as np
  23 | 
  24 | from pysr_harness.metrics import combined_score_from_nmse
  25 | 
  26 | DATA_FILE = BENCHMARK_DIR / "fit.tsv"
  27 | RANDOM_STATE = 42
  28 | TEST_SIZE = 0.25
  29 | 
  30 | 
  31 | def _concentration_from_column(column_name: str) -> float:
  32 |     """Extract concentration in uM from a response column label."""
  33 |     match = re.search(r":\s*([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)uM\s*$", column_name)
  34 |     if match is None:
  35 |         raise ValueError(f"Could not parse concentration from column: {column_name}")
  36 |     return float(match.group(1))
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def _load_fit_table(data_file: Path = DATA_FILE) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
  40 |     """Load wide fit.tsv and return X=[measurement_x, concentration_uM], y."""
  41 |     features: list[list[float]] = []
  42 |     targets: list[float] = []
  43 | 
  44 |     with data_file.open(newline="") as f:
  45 |         reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter="\t")
  46 |         header = next(reader)
  47 |         concentrations = [_concentration_from_column(name) for name in header[1:]]
  48 | 
  49 |         for row in reader:
  50 |             if not row:
  51 |                 continue
  52 |             measurement_x = float(row[0])
  53 |             for concentration, value in zip(concentrations, row[1:]):
  54 |                 if value == "" or value.strip().lower() == "nan":
  55 |                     continue
  56 |                 features.append([measurement_x, concentration])
  57 |                 targets.append(float(value))
  58 | 
  59 |     if not features:
  60 |         raise ValueError(f"No regression samples loaded from {data_file}")
  61 | 
  62 |     return np.asarray(features, dtype=float), np.asarray(targets, dtype=float)
  63 | 
  64 | 
  65 | def load_alphasyn_data():
  66 |     """Deterministic train/validation split for the copied Alpha-synuclein TSV."""
  67 |     X, y = _load_fit_table()
  68 |     rng = np.random.default_rng(RANDOM_STATE)
  69 |     indices = rng.permutation(len(y))
  70 |     split = int(round(len(y) * (1.0 - TEST_SIZE)))
  71 |     train_idx = indices[:split]
  72 |     val_idx = indices[split:]
  73 |     return X[train_idx], X[val_idx], y[train_idx], y[val_idx]
  74 | 
  75 | 
  76 | def evaluate_candidate_with_timeout(program_path: str, timeout_seconds: int = 300) -> dict:
  77 |     """
  78 |     Evaluate a candidate program in a subprocess and return its metrics dict.
  79 | 
  80 |     The candidate's `evaluate_symbolic_candidate()` function is the evolved
  81 |     artifact: it should build an equation template and call the harness evaluator.
  82 |     This function only isolates evaluation behind a timeout; it does not run
  83 |     PySR's search loop.
  84 |     """
  85 |     harness_root = str(BENCHMARK_ROOT)
  86 |     evaluator_path = str(Path(__file__).resolve())
  87 |     with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(suffix=".py", delete=False) as temp_file:
  88 |         script = f"""
  89 | import importlib.util
  90 | import pickle
  91 | import sys
  92 | import traceback
  93 | 
  94 | sys.path.insert(0, {harness_root!r})
  95 | 
  96 | program_path = {program_path!r}
  97 | evaluator_path = {evaluator_path!r}
  98 | results_path = {temp_file.name + ".results"!r}
  99 | 
 100 | try:
 101 |     evaluator_spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("benchmark_evaluator", evaluator_path)
 102 |     evaluator = importlib.util.module_from_spec(evaluator_spec)
 103 |     evaluator_spec.loader.exec_module(evaluator)
 104 | 
 105 |     spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("program", program_path)
 106 |     program = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
 107 |     spec.loader.exec_module(program)
 108 | 
 109 |     X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val = evaluator.load_alphasyn_data()
 110 | 
 111 |     if hasattr(program, "evaluate_symbolic_candidate"):
 112 |         result = program.evaluate_symbolic_candidate(
 113 |             X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val
 114 |         )
 115 |     elif hasattr(program, "run_discovery"):
 116 |         result = program.run_discovery(X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val)
 117 |     else:
 118 |         raise AttributeError("Program must define evaluate_symbolic_candidate() or run_discovery()")
 119 | 
 120 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 121 |         pickle.dump({{"result": result}}, f)
 122 | except Exception as exc:
 123 |     traceback.print_exc()
 124 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 125 |         pickle.dump({{"error": str(exc)}}, f)
 126 | """
 127 |         temp_file.write(script.encode())
 128 |         temp_path = temp_file.name
 129 | 
 130 |     results_path = f"{temp_path}.results"
 131 |     try:
 132 |         process = subprocess.Popen(
 133 |             [sys.executable, temp_path],
 134 |             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
 135 |             stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
 136 |         )
 137 |         stdout, stderr = process.communicate(timeout=timeout_seconds)
 138 |         if stdout:
 139 |             print(stdout.decode())
 140 |         if stderr:
 141 |             print(stderr.decode())
 142 |         if process.returncode != 0:
 143 |             raise RuntimeError(f"Subprocess exited with code {process.returncode}")
 144 |         if not os.path.exists(results_path):
 145 |             raise RuntimeError("Results file not found")
 146 |         with open(results_path, "rb") as f:
 147 |             payload = pickle.load(f)
 148 |         if "error" in payload:
 149 |             raise RuntimeError(payload["error"])
 150 |         return payload["result"]
 151 |     except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
 152 |         process.kill()
 153 |         process.wait()
 154 |         raise TimeoutError(f"Program execution timed out after {timeout_seconds}s")
 155 |     finally:
 156 |         for path in (temp_path, results_path):
 157 |             if os.path.exists(path):
 158 |                 os.unlink(path)
 159 | 
 160 | 
 161 | def _metrics_from_result(result: dict, eval_time: float) -> dict:
 162 |     """Normalize harness output into SkyDiscover evaluator metrics."""
 163 |     nmse_val = float(result.get("nmse_val", float("inf")))
 164 |     combined = float(result.get("combined_score", combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val)))
 165 |     if not np.isfinite(combined):
 166 |         combined = 0.0
 167 | 
 168 |     return {
 169 |         "equation": str(result.get("equation", "")),
 170 |         "loss": float(result.get("loss", float("inf"))),
 171 |         "complexity": float(result.get("complexity", 0.0)),
 172 |         "nmse_train": float(result.get("nmse_train", float("inf"))),
 173 |         "nmse_val": nmse_val,
 174 |         "combined_score": combined,
 175 |         "eval_time": float(eval_time),
 176 |     }
 177 | 
 178 | 
 179 | def evaluate(program_path: str) -> dict:
 180 |     """Evaluate one evolved symbolic-equation candidate on the Alpha-synuclein TSV."""
 181 |     try:
 182 |         start = time.time()
 183 |         result = evaluate_candidate_with_timeout(program_path, timeout_seconds=600)
 184 |         metrics = _metrics_from_result(result, time.time() - start)
 185 |         print(
 186 |             "Evaluation: "
 187 |             f"nmse_val={metrics['nmse_val']:.6f}, "
 188 |             f"complexity={metrics['complexity']:.1f}, "
 189 |             f"combined_score={metrics['combined_score']:.6f}, "
 190 |             f"time={metrics['eval_time']:.2f}s"
 191 |         )
 192 |         print(f"Best equation: {metrics['equation']}")
 193 |         return metrics
 194 |     except Exception as exc:
 195 |         print(f"Evaluation failed: {exc}")
 196 |         traceback.print_exc()
 197 |         return {
 198 |             "equation": "",
 199 |             "loss": float("inf"),
 200 |             "complexity": 0.0,
 201 |             "nmse_train": float("inf"),
 202 |             "nmse_val": float("inf"),
 203 |             "combined_score": 0.0,
 204 |             "eval_time": 0.0,
 205 |             "error": str(exc),
 206 |         }
 207 | 
 208 | 
 209 | def evaluate_stage1(program_path: str) -> dict:
 210 |     """Fast cascade stage for one evolved symbolic-equation candidate."""
 211 |     try:
 212 |         harness_root = str(BENCHMARK_ROOT)
 213 |         if harness_root not in sys.path:
 214 |             sys.path.insert(0, harness_root)
 215 | 
 216 |         spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("program", program_path)
 217 |         program = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
 218 |         spec.loader.exec_module(program)
 219 | 
 220 |         fn = getattr(program, "evaluate_symbolic_candidate", None) or getattr(
 221 |             program, "run_discovery", None
 222 |         )
 223 |         if fn is None:
 224 |             return {"combined_score": 0.0, "error": "missing evaluate_symbolic_candidate()"}
 225 | 
 226 |         X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val = load_alphasyn_data()
 227 |         n = min(300, len(X_train))
 228 |         m = min(120, len(X_val))
 229 | 
 230 |         start = time.time()
 231 |         result = fn(X_train[:n], y_train[:n], X_val[:m], y_val[:m])
 232 |         metrics = _metrics_from_result(result, time.time() - start)
 233 |         return metrics
 234 |     except Exception as exc:
 235 |         print(f"Stage 1 evaluation failed: {exc}")
 236 |         return {"combined_score": 0.0, "error": str(exc)}
 237 | 
 238 | 
 239 | def evaluate_stage2(program_path: str) -> dict:
 240 |     """Full evaluation for cascade stage 2."""
 241 |     return evaluate(program_path)
 242 | 
 243 | 
 244 | if __name__ == "__main__":
 245 |     default_program = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "initial_program.py"
 246 |     path = sys.argv[1] if len(sys.argv) > 1 else str(default_program)
 247 |     print(evaluate(path))

import csv
import numpy as np

with open('alphasyn_gaspar2017_03um_seed_all/fit.tsv') as f:
    reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
    header = next(reader)
    cols = header[1:]
    times = []
    rows = {c: [] for c in cols}
    for row in reader:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        times.append(t)
        for c, v in zip(cols, row[1:]):
            rows[c].append(float(v))

times = np.array(times)
# For each concentration, find the half-time (where y = 0.5 * max + 0.5 * min)
for c in cols:
    arr = np.array(rows[c])
    ymin, ymax = arr.min(), arr.max()
    ymid = (ymin + ymax) / 2
    # Find crossing
    idx = np.argmin(np.abs(arr - ymid))
    conc = float(c.split(':')[1].strip().replace('uM',''))
    print(f'C={conc:5.1f} uM: t_half~{times[idx]:.2f}h, ymin={ymin:.4f}, ymax={ymax:.4f}')
"

import csv
import numpy as np

with open('alphasyn_gaspar2017_03um_seed_all/fit.tsv') as f:
    reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
    header = next(reader)
    cols = header[1:]
    times = []
    rows = {c: [] for c in cols}
    for row in reader:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        times.append(t)
        for c, v in zip(cols, row[1:]):
            rows[c].append(float(v) if v.strip() not in ('', 'nan', 'NaN') else np.nan)

times = np.array(times)
for c in cols:
    arr = np.array(rows[c])
    valid = arr[~np.isnan(arr)]
    conc = float(c.split(':')[1].strip().replace('uM',''))
    if len(valid) > 0:
        ymid = (valid.min() + valid.max()) / 2
        t_valid = times[~np.isnan(arr)]
        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(valid - ymid))
        print(f'C={conc:5.1f} uM: t_half~{t_valid[idx]:.2f}h, ymin={valid.min():.4f}, ymax={valid.max():.4f}, n={len(valid)}')
    else:
        print(f'C={conc:5.1f} uM: no valid data')
"

  23 | @dataclass(frozen=True)
  24 | class FittedExpression:
  25 |     """A fitted symbolic expression and its validation predictions."""
  26 |

  33 | 
  34 | def feature_symbols(n_features: int) -> list[sp.Symbol]:
  35 |     """Create PySR-compatible feature symbols x0, x1, ..."""
  36 |     return create_sympy_symbols([f"x{i}" for i in range(n_features)])
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def constant_symbols(n_constants: int) -> list[sp.Symbol]:
  40 |     """Create tunable constant symbols c0, c1, ..."""
  41 |     return [sp.Symbol(f"c{i}", real=True) for i in range(n_constants)]
  42 | 
  43 | 
  44 | def pysr_operator_names() -> dict[str, list[str]]:
  45 |     """Return the PySR operator vocabulary exposed to evolved equation builders."""
  46 |     return {
  47 |         "unary": GENERAL_UNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  48 |         "binary": GENERAL_BINARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  49 |         "ternary": GENERAL_TERNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  50 |     }
  51 | 
  52 | 
  53 | def pysr_operator_namespace() -> dict[str, Any]:
  54 |     """
  55 |     Return PySR-to-SymPy operator callables usable in expression templates.
  56 | 
  57 |     Operators like ``+``, ``-``, ``*``, and ``/`` should be written with normal
  58 |     Python syntax. Named PySR operators such as ``sin``, ``cos``, ``sqrt``,
  59 |     ``log1p``, ``max``, ``min``, ``muladd``, and ``clamp`` are exposed here.
  60 |     """
  61 |     return {
  62 |         **sympy_mappings,
  63 |         "pi": sp.pi,
  64 |         "E": sp.E,
  65 |     }
  66 | 
  67 | 
  68 | def _as_sympy_expr(expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> sp.Expr:
  69 |     if isinstance(expression, sp.Expr):

  71 |     return pysr2sympy(expression, feature_names_in=list(feature_names))
  72 | 
  73 | 
  74 | def _complexity(expression: sp.Expr) -> float:
  75 |     return float(sum(1 for _ in sp.preorder_traversal(expression)))
  76 | 
  77 | 
  78 | def _predict(expression: sp.Expr, X: NDArray, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> NDArray:
  79 |     symbols = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
  80 |     fn = sympy2numpy(expression, symbols)
  81 |     with np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):

  83 |             y_pred = fn(np.asarray(X, dtype=float))
  84 |         else:
  85 |             y_pred = fn(*[X[:, i] for i in range(X.shape[1])])
  86 |     return np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
  87 | 
  88 | 
  89 | def fit_expression_constants(
  90 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
  91 |     X_train: NDArray,
  92 |     y_train: NDArray,
  93 |     X_val: NDArray,
  94 |     *,
  95 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
  96 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
  97 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
  98 | ) -> FittedExpression:
  99 |     """
 100 |     Fit free constants in a SkyDiscover-proposed expression template.
 101 | 
 102 |     The expression structure is supplied by the evolved program. This helper only
 103 |     performs the continuous inner fit and PySR-style export/evaluation.
 104 |     """
 105 |     X_train = np.asarray(X_train, dtype=float)
 106 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 107 |     X_val = np.asarray(X_val, dtype=float)
 108 |     feature_names = [f"x{i}" for i in range(X_train.shape[1])]
 109 |     template = _as_sympy_expr(expression, feature_names)
 110 | 
 111 |     if constants is None:
 112 |         feature_set = set(feature_symbols(X_train.shape[1]))
 113 |         constants = sorted(template.free_symbols - feature_set, key=lambda s: s.name)
 114 |     constants = list(constants)
 115 | 
 116 |     if not constants:
 117 |         fitted_expr = sp.simplify(template)
 118 |         return FittedExpression(
 119 |             expression_template=template,
 120 |             expression=fitted_expr,
 121 |             constants={},
 122 |             y_pred_train=_predict(fitted_expr, X_train, feature_names),
 123 |             y_pred_val=_predict(fitted_expr, X_val, feature_names),
 124 |         )
 125 | 
 126 |     if initial_values is None:
 127 |         x0 = np.ones(len(constants), dtype=float)
 128 |     else:
 129 |         x0 = np.asarray(initial_values, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 130 |         if x0.size != len(constants):
 131 |             raise ValueError("initial_values must match the number of constants")
 132 | 
 133 |     def residual(theta: NDArray) -> NDArray:
 134 |         substitutions = {symbol: float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, theta)}
 135 |         candidate = template.subs(substitutions)
 136 |         try:
 137 |             prediction = _predict(candidate, X_train, feature_names)
 138 |         except Exception:
 139 |             return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 140 |         if prediction.shape != y_train.shape or not np.all(np.isfinite(prediction)):
 141 |             return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 142 |         return prediction - y_train
 143 | 
 144 |     import warnings
 145 | 
 146 |     with warnings.catch_warnings(), np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
 147 |         warnings.simplefilter("ignore", RuntimeWarning)
 148 |         result = least_squares(
 149 |             residual,
 150 |             x0,
 151 |             loss="soft_l1",
 152 |             max_nfev=max_nfev,
 153 |         )
 154 |     fitted_constants = {
 155 |         str(symbol): float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, result.x)
 156 |     }
 157 |     substitutions = dict(zip(constants, result.x))
 158 |     fitted_expr = sp.simplify(template.subs(substitutions))
 159 | 
 160 |     return FittedExpression(
 161 |         expression_template=template,
 162 |         expression=fitted_expr,
 163 |         constants=fitted_constants,
 164 |         y_pred_train=_predict(fitted_expr, X_train, feature_names),
 165 |         y_pred_val=_predict(fitted_expr, X_val, feature_names),
 166 |     )
 167 | 
 168 | 
 169 | def evaluate_expression(
 170 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
 171 |     X_train: NDArray,
 172 |     y_train: NDArray,
 173 |     X_val: NDArray,
 174 |     y_val: NDArray,
 175 |     *,
 176 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
 177 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
 178 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
 179 | ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 180 |     """Score a proposed equation template after fitting its constants."""
 181 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 182 |     y_val = np.asarray(y_val, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 183 |     fitted = fit_expression_constants(
 184 |         expression,
 185 |         X_train,
 186 |         y_train,
 187 |         X_val,
 188 |         constants=constants,
 189 |         initial_values=initial_values,
 190 |         max_nfev=max_nfev,
 191 |     )
 192 |     nmse_train = nmse(y_train, fitted.y_pred_train)
 193 |     nmse_val = nmse(y_val, fitted.y_pred_val)
 194 |     loss = float(np.mean((fitted.y_pred_train - y_train) ** 2))
 195 | 
 196 |     return {
 197 |         "equation_template": str(fitted.expression_template),
 198 |         "equation": str(fitted.expression),
 199 |         "constants": fitted.constants,
 200 |         "loss": loss,
 201 |         "complexity": _complexity(fitted.expression_template),
 202 |         "nmse_train": nmse_train,
 203 |         "nmse_val": nmse_val,
 204 |         "combined_score": combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val),

   1 | """Shared scoring helpers for symbolic regression benchmarks."""

   3 | from __future__ import annotations
   4 | 
   5 | import numpy as np
   6 | from numpy.typing import NDArray

   8 | 
   9 | def nmse(y_true: NDArray, y_pred: NDArray) -> float:
  10 |     """Normalized mean squared error."""
  11 |     y_true = np.asarray(y_true, dtype=float).ravel()
  12 |     y_pred = np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).ravel()
  13 |     if y_true.shape != y_pred.shape:
  14 |         return float("inf")
  15 |     if not np.all(np.isfinite(y_pred)):
  16 |         return float("inf")
  17 |     var = float(np.var(y_true))
  18 |     if var <= 0.0:
  19 |         return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2))
  20 |     return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2) / var)
  21 | 
  22 | 
  23 | def combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val: float) -> float:
  24 |     """Higher is better; zero for invalid or infinite NMSE."""
  25 |     if not np.isfinite(nmse_val):
  26 |         return 0.0
  27 |     return float(1.0 / (1.0 + max(nmse_val, 0.0)))

  30 | 
  31 | def _concentration_from_column(column_name: str) -> float:
  32 |     """Extract concentration in uM from a response column label."""
  33 |     match = re.search(r":\s*([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)uM\s*$", column_name)
  34 |     if match is None:
  35 |         raise ValueError(f"Could not parse concentration from column: {column_name}")
  36 |     return float(match.group(1))
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def _load_fit_table(data_file: Path = DATA_FILE) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
  40 |     """Load wide fit.tsv and return X=[measurement_x, concentration_uM], y."""
  41 |     features: list[list[float]] = []
  42 |     targets: list[float] = []
  43 | 
  44 |     with data_file.open(newline="") as f:
  45 |         reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter="\t")
  46 |         header = next(reader)
  47 |         concentrations = [_concentration_from_column(name) for name in header[1:]]
  48 | 
  49 |         for row in reader:
  50 |             if not row:
  51 |                 continue
  52 |             measurement_x = float(row[0])
  53 |             for concentration, value in zip(concentrations, row[1:]):
  54 |                 if value == "" or value.strip().lower() == "nan":
  55 |                     continue
  56 |                 features.append([measurement_x, concentration])
  57 |                 targets.append(float(value))
  58 | 
  59 |     if not features:
  60 |         raise ValueError(f"No regression samples loaded from {data_file}")
  61 | 
  62 |     return np.asarray(features, dtype=float), np.asarray(targets, dtype=float)
  63 | 
  64 | 
  65 | def load_alphasyn_data():
  66 |     """Deterministic train/validation split for the copied Alpha-synuclein TSV."""
  67 |     X, y = _load_fit_table()
  68 |     rng = np.random.default_rng(RANDOM_STATE)
  69 |     indices = rng.permutation(len(y))
  70 |     split = int(round(len(y) * (1.0 - TEST_SIZE)))
  71 |     train_idx = indices[:split]
  72 |     val_idx = indices[split:]
  73 |     return X[train_idx], X[val_idx], y[train_idx], y[val_idx]
  74 |

  76 | def evaluate_candidate_with_timeout(program_path: str, timeout_seconds: int = 300) -> dict:
  77 |     """
  78 |     Evaluate a candidate program in a subprocess and return its metrics dict.
  79 | 
  80 |     The candidate's `evaluate_symbolic_candidate()` function is the evolved
  81 |     artifact: it should build an equation template and call the harness evaluator.
  82 |     This function only isolates evaluation behind a timeout; it does not run
  83 |     PySR's search loop.
  84 |     """
  85 |     harness_root = str(BENCHMARK_ROOT)
  86 |     evaluator_path = str(Path(__file__).resolve())
  87 |     with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(suffix=".py", delete=False) as temp_file:

  90 | import pickle
  91 | import sys
  92 | import traceback
  93 | 
  94 | sys.path.insert(0, {harness_root!r})
  95 |

 104 |

 106 |     program = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
 107 |     spec.loader.exec_module(program)

 109 |     X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val = evaluator.load_alphasyn_data()
 110 | 
 111 |     if hasattr(program, "evaluate_symbolic_candidate"):
 112 |         result = program.evaluate_symbolic_candidate(
 113 |             X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val
 114 |         )
 115 |     elif hasattr(program, "run_discovery"):
 116 |         result = program.run_discovery(X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val)
 117 |     else:
 118 |         raise AttributeError("Program must define evaluate_symbolic_candidate() or run_discovery()")
 119 | 
 120 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 121 |         pickle.dump({{"result": result}}, f)
 122 | except Exception as exc:
 123 |     traceback.print_exc()
 124 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 125 |         pickle.dump({{"error": str(exc)}}, f)
 126 | """
 127 |         temp_file.write(script.encode())
 128 |         temp_path = temp_file.name
 129 | 
 130 |     results_path = f"{temp_path}.results"
 131 |     try:
 132 |         process = subprocess.Popen(
 133 |             [sys.executable, temp_path],
 134 |             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
 135 |             stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
 136 |         )
 137 |         stdout, stderr = process.communicate(timeout=timeout_seconds)
 138 |         if stdout:
 139 |             print(stdout.decode())
 140 |         if stderr:
 141 |             print(stderr.decode())
 142 |         if process.returncode != 0:
 143 |             raise RuntimeError(f"Subprocess exited with code {process.returncode}")
 144 |         if not os.path.exists(results_path):
 145 |             raise RuntimeError("Results file not found")
 146 |         with open(results_path, "rb") as f:
 147 |             payload = pickle.load(f)
 148 |         if "error" in payload:
 149 |             raise RuntimeError(payload["error"])
 150 |         return payload["result"]
 151 |     except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
 152 |         process.kill()
 153 |         process.wait()
 154 |         raise TimeoutError(f"Program execution timed out after {timeout_seconds}s")
 155 |     finally:
 156 |         for path in (temp_path, results_path):
 157 |             if os.path.exists(path):
 158 |                 os.unlink(path)

import csv
import numpy as np

data = []
with open('alphasyn_gaspar2017_03um_seed_all/fit.tsv') as f:
    reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
    header = next(reader)
    for row in reader:
        if row:
            data.append([float(x) if x else float('nan') for x in row])

data = np.array(data)
times = data[:, 0]
concs = [1,2,3,5,10,20,30,50]

# Find the half-time (t where y=0.5) for each concentration
print('Half-times and initial values for each concentration:')
for i, c in enumerate(concs):
    col = data[:, i+1]
    y0 = col[0]
    # find t_half
    above = np.where(col >= 0.5)[0]
    if len(above) > 0:
        idx = above[0]
        t_half = times[idx]

        t_half = float('nan')

  23 | @dataclass(frozen=True)
  24 | class FittedExpression:
  25 |     """A fitted symbolic expression and its validation predictions."""

  34 | def feature_symbols(n_features: int) -> list[sp.Symbol]:
  35 |     """Create PySR-compatible feature symbols x0, x1, ..."""
  36 |     return create_sympy_symbols([f"x{i}" for i in range(n_features)])
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def constant_symbols(n_constants: int) -> list[sp.Symbol]:
  40 |     """Create tunable constant symbols c0, c1, ..."""
  41 |     return [sp.Symbol(f"c{i}", real=True) for i in range(n_constants)]
  42 | 
  43 | 
  44 | def pysr_operator_names() -> dict[str, list[str]]:
  45 |     """Return the PySR operator vocabulary exposed to evolved equation builders."""
  46 |     return {
  47 |         "unary": GENERAL_UNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  48 |         "binary": GENERAL_BINARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  49 |         "ternary": GENERAL_TERNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  50 |     }
  51 | 
  52 | 
  53 | def pysr_operator_namespace() -> dict[str, Any]:
  54 |     """
  55 |     Return PySR-to-SymPy operator callables usable in expression templates.
  56 | 
  57 |     Operators like ``+``, ``-``, ``*``, and ``/`` should be written with normal
  58 |     Python syntax. Named PySR operators such as ``sin``, ``cos``, ``sqrt``,
  59 |     ``log1p``, ``max``, ``min``, ``muladd``, and ``clamp`` are exposed here.
  60 |     """
  61 |     return {
  62 |         **sympy_mappings,
  63 |         "pi": sp.pi,
  64 |         "E": sp.E,
  65 |     }
  66 | 
  67 | 
  68 | def _as_sympy_expr(expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> sp.Expr:
  69 |     if isinstance(expression, sp.Expr):
  70 |         return expression
  71 |     return pysr2sympy(expression, feature_names_in=list(feature_names))
  72 | 
  73 | 
  74 | def _complexity(expression: sp.Expr) -> float:
  75 |     return float(sum(1 for _ in sp.preorder_traversal(expression)))
  76 | 
  77 | 
  78 | def _predict(expression: sp.Expr, X: NDArray, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> NDArray:
  79 |     symbols = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
  80 |     fn = sympy2numpy(expression, symbols)
  81 |     with np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
  82 |         if isinstance(fn, CallableEquation):
  83 |             y_pred = fn(np.asarray(X, dtype=float))
  84 |         else:
  85 |             y_pred = fn(*[X[:, i] for i in range(X.shape[1])])
  86 |     return np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
  87 | 
  88 | 
  89 | def fit_expression_constants(
  90 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
  91 |     X_train: NDArray,
  92 |     y_train: NDArray,
  93 |     X_val: NDArray,
  94 |     *,
  95 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
  96 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
  97 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
  98 | ) -> FittedExpression:
  99 |     """
 100 |     Fit free constants in a SkyDiscover-proposed expression template.
 101 | 
 102 |     The expression structure is supplied by the evolved program. This helper only
 103 |     performs the continuous inner fit and PySR-style export/evaluation.
 104 |     """
 105 |     X_train = np.asarray(X_train, dtype=float)
 106 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 107 |     X_val = np.asarray(X_val, dtype=float)
 108 |     feature_names = [f"x{i}" for i in range(X_train.shape[1])]
 109 |     template = _as_sympy_expr(expression, feature_names)
 110 | 
 111 |     if constants is None:
 112 |         feature_set = set(feature_symbols(X_train.shape[1]))
 113 |         constants = sorted(template.free_symbols - feature_set, key=lambda s: s.name)
 114 |     constants = list(constants)
 115 | 
 116 |     if not constants:
 117 |         fitted_expr = sp.simplify(template)
 118 |         return FittedExpression(
 119 |             expression_template=template,
 120 |             expression=fitted_expr,
 121 |             constants={},
 122 |             y_pred_train=_predict(fitted_expr, X_train, feature_names),
 123 |             y_pred_val=_predict(fitted_expr, X_val, feature_names),
 124 |         )
 125 | 
 126 |     if initial_values is None:
 127 |         x0 = np.ones(len(constants), dtype=float)
 128 |     else:
 129 |         x0 = np.asarray(initial_values, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 130 |         if x0.size != len(constants):
 131 |             raise ValueError("initial_values must match the number of constants")
 132 | 
 133 |     def residual(theta: NDArray) -> NDArray:
 134 |         substitutions = {symbol: float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, theta)}
 135 |         candidate = template.subs(substitutions)
 136 |         try:
 137 |             prediction = _predict(candidate, X_train, feature_names)
 138 |         except Exception:
 139 |             return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 140 |         if prediction.shape != y_train.shape or not np.all(np.isfinite(prediction)):
 141 |             return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 142 |         return prediction - y_train
 143 | 
 144 |     import warnings
 145 | 
 146 |     with warnings.catch_warnings(), np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
 147 |         warnings.simplefilter("ignore", RuntimeWarning)
 148 |         result = least_squares(
 149 |             residual,
 150 |             x0,
 151 |             loss="soft_l1",
 152 |             max_nfev=max_nfev,
 153 |         )
 154 |     fitted_constants = {
 155 |         str(symbol): float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, result.x)
 156 |     }
 157 |     substitutions = dict(zip(constants, result.x))
 158 |     fitted_expr = sp.simplify(template.subs(substitutions))
 159 | 
 160 |     return FittedExpression(
 161 |         expression_template=template,
 162 |         expression=fitted_expr,
 163 |         constants=fitted_constants,
 164 |         y_pred_train=_predict(fitted_expr, X_train, feature_names),
 165 |         y_pred_val=_predict(fitted_expr, X_val, feature_names),
 166 |     )
 167 | 
 168 | 
 169 | def evaluate_expression(
 170 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
 171 |     X_train: NDArray,
 172 |     y_train: NDArray,
 173 |     X_val: NDArray,
 174 |     y_val: NDArray,
 175 |     *,
 176 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
 177 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
 178 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
 179 | ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 180 |     """Score a proposed equation template after fitting its constants."""
 181 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 182 |     y_val = np.asarray(y_val, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 183 |     fitted = fit_expression_constants(
 184 |         expression,
 185 |         X_train,

 187 |         X_val,
 188 |         constants=constants,
 189 |         initial_values=initial_values,
 190 |         max_nfev=max_nfev,
 191 |     )
 192 |     nmse_train = nmse(y_train, fitted.y_pred_train)
 193 |     nmse_val = nmse(y_val, fitted.y_pred_val)
 194 |     loss = float(np.mean((fitted.y_pred_train - y_train) ** 2))
 195 | 
 196 |     return {
 197 |         "equation_template": str(fitted.expression_template),
 198 |         "equation": str(fitted.expression),
 199 |         "constants": fitted.constants,
 200 |         "loss": loss,
 201 |         "complexity": _complexity(fitted.expression_template),

 204 |         "combined_score": combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val),

   3 | from __future__ import annotations

   9 | def nmse(y_true: NDArray, y_pred: NDArray) -> float:
  10 |     """Normalized mean squared error."""
  11 |     y_true = np.asarray(y_true, dtype=float).ravel()
  12 |     y_pred = np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).ravel()
  13 |     if y_true.shape != y_pred.shape:
  14 |         return float("inf")
  15 |     if not np.all(np.isfinite(y_pred)):
  16 |         return float("inf")
  17 |     var = float(np.var(y_true))
  18 |     if var <= 0.0:
  19 |         return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2))
  20 |     return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2) / var)
  21 | 
  22 | 
  23 | def combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val: float) -> float:
  24 |     """Higher is better; zero for invalid or infinite NMSE."""
  25 |     if not np.isfinite(nmse_val):
  26 |         return 0.0
  27 |     return float(1.0 / (1.0 + max(nmse_val, 0.0)))

  31 | def _concentration_from_column(column_name: str) -> float:
  32 |     """Extract concentration in uM from a response column label."""
  33 |     match = re.search(r":\s*([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)uM\s*$", column_name)
  34 |     if match is None:
  35 |         raise ValueError(f"Could not parse concentration from column: {column_name}")
  36 |     return float(match.group(1))
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def _load_fit_table(data_file: Path = DATA_FILE) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
  40 |     """Load wide fit.tsv and return X=[measurement_x, concentration_uM], y."""
  41 |     features: list[list[float]] = []
  42 |     targets: list[float] = []
  43 | 
  44 |     with data_file.open(newline="") as f:
  45 |         reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter="\t")
  46 |         header = next(reader)
  47 |         concentrations = [_concentration_from_column(name) for name in header[1:]]
  48 | 
  49 |         for row in reader:
  50 |             if not row:
  51 |                 continue
  52 |             measurement_x = float(row[0])
  53 |             for concentration, value in zip(concentrations, row[1:]):
  54 |                 if value == "" or value.strip().lower() == "nan":
  55 |                     continue
  56 |                 features.append([measurement_x, concentration])
  57 |                 targets.append(float(value))
  58 | 
  59 |     if not features:
  60 |         raise ValueError(f"No regression samples loaded from {data_file}")
  61 | 
  62 |     return np.asarray(features, dtype=float), np.asarray(targets, dtype=float)
  63 | 
  64 | 
  65 | def load_alphasyn_data():
  66 |     """Deterministic train/validation split for the copied Alpha-synuclein TSV."""
  67 |     X, y = _load_fit_table()
  68 |     rng = np.random.default_rng(RANDOM_STATE)
  69 |     indices = rng.permutation(len(y))
  70 |     split = int(round(len(y) * (1.0 - TEST_SIZE)))
  71 |     train_idx = indices[:split]
  72 |     val_idx = indices[split:]
  73 |     return X[train_idx], X[val_idx], y[train_idx], y[val_idx]
  74 | 
  75 |

 124 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:

 129 | 
 130 |     results_path = f"{temp_path}.results"
 131 |     try:
 132 |         process = subprocess.Popen(

 134 |             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
 135 |             stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
 136 |         )
 137 |         stdout, stderr = process.communicate(timeout=timeout_seconds)

 152 |         process.kill()
 153 |         process.wait()

 161 | def _metrics_from_result(result: dict, eval_time: float) -> dict:
 162 |     """Normalize harness output into SkyDiscover evaluator metrics."""
 163 |     nmse_val = float(result.get("nmse_val", float("inf")))

 174 |         "combined_score": combined,

import csv
import numpy as np

with open('alphasyn_gaspar2017_03um_seed_all/fit.tsv') as f:
    reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
    header = next(reader)
    import re
    concentrations = []
    for name in header[1:]:
        m = re.search(r':\s*([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)uM', name)
        concentrations.append(float(m.group(1)))
    
    rows = []
    for row in reader:
        if not row: continue
        rows.append([float(x) if x and x.strip().lower() != 'nan' else np.nan for x in row])

data = np.array(rows)
print('Time range:', data[:,0].min(), data[:,0].max())
print('Concentrations:', concentrations)
print('Data shape:', data.shape)

# Check which concentrations have NaN
for ci, c in enumerate(concentrations):
    vals = data[:, ci+1]
    nan_count = np.sum(np.isnan(vals))
    valid = vals[~np.isnan(vals)]
    if len(valid) > 0:
        t50_idx = np.argmin(np.abs(valid - 0.5))
        times = data[:,0][~np.isnan(vals)]
        print(f'C={c}uM: NaN={nan_count}, min={np.nanmin(vals):.4f}, max={np.nanmax(vals):.4f}, t_half~{times[t50_idx]:.2f}')
    else:
        print(f'C={c}uM: all NaN')

import csv
import numpy as np

with open('alphasyn_gaspar2017_03um_seed_all/fit.tsv') as f:
    reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
    header = next(reader)
    import re
    concentrations = []
    for name in header[1:]:
        m = re.search(r':\s*([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)uM', name)
        concentrations.append(float(m.group(1)))
    
    rows = []
    for row in reader:
        if not row: continue
        rows.append([float(x) if x and x.strip().lower() != 'nan' else np.nan for x in row])

data = np.array(rows)

# The half-times are all around 9 hours and don't change much with concentration
# This is interesting - let's look at the initial values and the shape more carefully
print('Initial values (t=0) for each concentration:')
for ci, c in enumerate(concentrations):
    print(f'  C={c}uM: y(0)={data[0, ci+1]:.4f}')

import csv
import numpy as np
from scipy.optimize import curve_fit

with open('alphasyn_gaspar2017_03um_seed_all/fit.tsv') as f:
    reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
    header = next(reader)
    import re
    concentrations = []
    for name in header[1:]:
        m = re.search(r':\s*([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)uM', name)
        concentrations.append(float(m.group(1)))
    
    rows = []
    for row in reader:
        if not row: continue
        rows.append([float(x) if x and x.strip().lower() != 'nan' else np.nan for x in row])

data = np.array(rows)
times = data[:,0]

# Initial y(0) ~ seed_conc / (seed_conc + monomer_conc)
# = 0.3 / (0.3 + C) since seed is 0.3 uM
print('y(0) vs 0.3/(0.3+C):')
for ci, c in enumerate(concentrations):
    y0 = data[0, ci+1]
    model = 0.3 / (0.3 + c)
    print(f'  C={c}uM: y(0)={y0:.4f}, 0.3/(0.3+C)={model:.4f}, ratio={y0/model:.4f}')

print()
# Let's try fitting each curve individually with a logistic
from scipy.optimize import curve_fit

def logistic(t, k, t_half):
    return 1.0 / (1.0 + np.exp(-k * (t - t_half)))

print('Individual logistic fits:')
for ci, c in enumerate(concentrations):
    vals = data[:, ci+1]
    mask = ~np.isnan(vals)
    t_fit = times[mask]
    y_fit = vals[mask]
    try:
        popt, _ = curve_fit(logistic, t_fit, y_fit, p0=[0.5, 9.0], maxfev=10000)
        print(f'  C={c}uM: k={popt[0]:.4f}, t_half={popt[1]:.4f}')
    except Exception as e:
        print(f'  C={c}uM: FAILED {e}')

  57 |     Operators like ``+``, ``-``, ``*``, and ``/`` should be written with normal

  78 | def _predict(expression: sp.Expr, X: NDArray, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> NDArray:
  79 |     symbols = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
  80 |     fn = sympy2numpy(expression, symbols)
  81 |     with np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):

 125 | 
 126 |     if initial_values is None:
 127 |         x0 = np.ones(len(constants), dtype=float)
 128 |     else:

 130 |         if x0.size != len(constants):

pysr_harness/metrics.py (lines 1-27 of 27)
   1 | """Shared scoring helpers for symbolic regression benchmarks."""
   2 | 
   3 | from __future__ import annotations
   4 | 
   5 | import numpy as np
   6 | from numpy.typing import NDArray
   7 | 
   8 | 
   9 | def nmse(y_true: NDArray, y_pred: NDArray) -> float:
  10 |     """Normalized mean squared error."""
  11 |     y_true = np.asarray(y_true, dtype=float).ravel()
  12 |     y_pred = np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).ravel()
  13 |     if y_true.shape != y_pred.shape:
  14 |         return float("inf")
  15 |     if not np.all(np.isfinite(y_pred)):
  16 |         return float("inf")
  17 |     var = float(np.var(y_true))
  18 |     if var <= 0.0:
  19 |         return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2))
  20 |     return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2) / var)
  21 | 
  22 | 
  23 | def combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val: float) -> float:
  24 |     """Higher is better; zero for invalid or infinite NMSE."""
  25 |     if not np.isfinite(nmse_val):
  26 |         return 0.0
  27 |     return float(1.0 / (1.0 + max(nmse_val, 0.0)))

  31 | def _concentration_from_column(column_name: str) -> float:
  32 |     """Extract concentration in uM from a response column label."""
  33 |     match = re.search(r":\s*([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)uM\s*$", column_name)
  34 |     if match is None:
  35 |         raise ValueError(f"Could not parse concentration from column: {column_name}")
  36 |     return float(match.group(1))
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def _load_fit_table(data_file: Path = DATA_FILE) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
  40 |     """Load wide fit.tsv and return X=[measurement_x, concentration_uM], y."""
  41 |     features: list[list[float]] = []
  42 |     targets: list[float] = []
  43 | 
  44 |     with data_file.open(newline="") as f:
  45 |         reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter="\t")
  46 |         header = next(reader)
  47 |         concentrations = [_concentration_from_column(name) for name in header[1:]]
  48 |

  50 |             if not row:
  51 |                 continue
  52 |             measurement_x = float(row[0])
  53 |             for concentration, value in zip(concentrations, row[1:]):
  54 |                 if value == "" or value.strip().lower() == "nan":
  55 |                     continue
  56 |                 features.append([measurement_x, concentration])
  57 |                 targets.append(float(value))
  58 | 
  59 |     if not features:
  60 |         raise ValueError(f"No regression samples loaded from {data_file}")
  61 | 
  62 |     return np.asarray(features, dtype=float), np.asarray(targets, dtype=float)
  63 | 
  64 | 
  65 | def load_alphasyn_data():
  66 |     """Deterministic train/validation split for the copied Alpha-synuclein TSV."""
  67 |     X, y = _load_fit_table()
  68 |     rng = np.random.default_rng(RANDOM_STATE)
  69 |     indices = rng.permutation(len(y))
  70 |     split = int(round(len(y) * (1.0 - TEST_SIZE)))
  71 |     train_idx = indices[:split]
  72 |     val_idx = indices[split:]
  73 |     return X[train_idx], X[val_idx], y[train_idx], y[val_idx]
  74 | 
  75 | 
  76 | def evaluate_candidate_with_timeout(program_path: str, timeout_seconds: int = 300) -> dict:
  77 |     """
  78 |     Evaluate a candidate program in a subprocess and return its metrics dict.
  79 | 
  80 |     The candidate's `evaluate_symbolic_candidate()` function is the evolved
  81 |     artifact: it should build an equation template and call the harness evaluator.
  82 |     This function only isolates evaluation behind a timeout; it does not run
  83 |     PySR's search loop.
  84 |     """
  85 |     harness_root = str(BENCHMARK_ROOT)
  86 |     evaluator_path = str(Path(__file__).resolve())
  87 |     with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(suffix=".py", delete=False) as temp_file:
  88 |         script = f"""
  89 | import importlib.util
  90 | import pickle
  91 | import sys
  92 | import traceback
  93 | 
  94 | sys.path.insert(0, {harness_root!r})
  95 | 
  96 | program_path = {program_path!r}
  97 | evaluator_path = {evaluator_path!r}
  98 | results_path = {temp_file.name + ".results"!r}
  99 | 
 100 | try:
 101 |     evaluator_spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("benchmark_evaluator", evaluator_path)
 102 |     evaluator = importlib.util.module_from_spec(evaluator_spec)
 103 |     evaluator_spec.loader.exec_module(evaluator)
 104 | 
 105 |     spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("program", program_path)
 106 |     program = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
 107 |     spec.loader.exec_module(program)
 108 | 
 109 |     X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val = evaluator.load_alphasyn_data()
 110 | 
 111 |     if hasattr(program, "evaluate_symbolic_candidate"):
 112 |         result = program.evaluate_symbolic_candidate(
 113 |             X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val
 114 |         )
 115 |     elif hasattr(program, "run_discovery"):
 116 |         result = program.run_discovery(X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val)
 117 |     else:
 118 |         raise AttributeError("Program must define evaluate_symbolic_candidate() or run_discovery()")
 119 | 
 120 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 121 |         pickle.dump({{"result": result}}, f)
 122 | except Exception as exc:
 123 |     traceback.print_exc()
 124 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 125 |         pickle.dump({{"error": str(exc)}}, f)
 126 | """
 127 |         temp_file.write(script.encode())
 128 |         temp_path = temp_file.name
 129 | 
 130 |     results_path = f"{temp_path}.results"
 131 |     try:
 132 |         process = subprocess.Popen(
 133 |             [sys.executable, temp_path],
 134 |             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
 135 |             stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
 136 |         )
 137 |         stdout, stderr = process.communicate(timeout=timeout_seconds)
 138 |         if stdout:
 139 |             print(stdout.decode())
 140 |         if stderr:
 141 |             print(stderr.decode())
 142 |         if process.returncode != 0:
 143 |             raise RuntimeError(f"Subprocess exited with code {process.returncode}")
 144 |         if not os.path.exists(results_path):
 145 |             raise RuntimeError("Results file not found")
 146 |         with open(results_path, "rb") as f:
 147 |             payload = pickle.load(f)
 148 |         if "error" in payload:
 149 |             raise RuntimeError(payload["error"])
 150 |         return payload["result"]
 151 |     except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
 152 |         process.kill()
 153 |         process.wait()
 154 |         raise TimeoutError(f"Program execution timed out after {timeout_seconds}s")
 155 |     finally:
 156 |         for path in (temp_path, results_path):
 157 |             if os.path.exists(path):
 158 |                 os.unlink(path)
 159 | 
 160 | 
 161 | def _metrics_from_result(result: dict, eval_time: float) -> dict:
 162 |     """Normalize harness output into SkyDiscover evaluator metrics."""
 163 |     nmse_val = float(result.get("nmse_val", float("inf")))
 164 |     combined = float(result.get("combined_score", combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val)))
 165 |     if not np.isfinite(combined):
 166 |         combined = 0.0
 167 | 
 168 |     return {
 169 |         "equation": str(result.get("equation", "")),
 170 |         "loss": float(result.get("loss", float("inf"))),
 171 |         "complexity": float(result.get("complexity", 0.0)),
 172 |         "nmse_train": float(result.get("nmse_train", float("inf"))),
 173 |         "nmse_val": nmse_val,
 174 |         "combined_score": combined,
 175 |         "eval_time": float(eval_time),
 176 |     }
 177 | 
 178 | 
 179 | def evaluate(program_path: str) -> dict:
 180 |     """Evaluate one evolved symbolic-equation candidate on the Alpha-synuclein TSV."""
 181 |     try:
 182 |         start = time.time()
 183 |         result = evaluate_candidate_with_timeout(program_path, timeout_seconds=600)
 184 |         metrics = _metrics_from_result(result, time.time() - start)
 185 |         print(
 186 |             "Evaluation: "
 187 |             f"nmse_val={metrics['nmse_val']:.6f}, "
 188 |             f"complexity={metrics['complexity']:.1f}, "
 189 |             f"combined_score={metrics['combined_score']:.6f}, "
 190 |             f"time={metrics['eval_time']:.2f}s"
 191 |         )
 192 |         print(f"Best equation: {metrics['equation']}")
 193 |         return metrics
 194 |     except Exception as exc:
 195 |         print(f"Evaluation failed: {exc}")
 196 |         traceback.print_exc()
 197 |         return {
 198 |             "equation": "",
 199 |             "loss": float("inf"),
 200 |             "complexity": 0.0,
 201 |             "nmse_train": float("inf"),

 204 |             "eval_time": 0.0,
 205 |             "error": str(exc),
 206 |         }
